Free Talk

Miscellaneous Notes

From Love to Magical Herbs 91

— Zhan Lu

Love is originally a beautiful word, but unfortunately, only a few get a happy ending from transformed love. For the sake of passionate love, unfortunate events occur, and for the sake of unrequited love, declarations of separation from marriage have become commonplace in daily newspapers. What is the reason for this?

The river of love is full of waves, and good things are often thwarted. This is common in the process of love and is not surprising. However, recent love tragedies are mostly due to unfaithfulness, becoming victims under triangular love, and cannot be attributed to fate, saying that the river of love is full of waves, and good things are often thwarted. To remedy these shortcomings in society, one is to prevent unfortunate events from occurring due to passionate love, and the other is to prevent men and women from separating due to unrequited love. Let alone moralists or politicians of the first rank, who are unable to influence or prohibit, can only take a deep breath and politely decline. Inadvertently, I found records of "Parting Love Grass" and "Harmonious Love Grass" in the *Compendium of Materia Medica Supplement*. A mere blade of grass can control the separation and union of love between men and women. This is truly a magical herb for saving society and a remedy for passionate love and unrequited love. I have listed the origin and efficacy of the two herbs below:

Parting Love Grass is produced in the Yi region of Yunnan. Many civilians sell it. When people are imprisoned by emotions and desires, they often die. If you take a blade of this grass and decoct it, you will immediately wake up as if from a dream, severing ties and abandoning love, without even knowing why.

Harmonious Love Grass is produced outside the Lancang River in Yongchang Prefecture. The roots of the grass are pure white, forming the shape of men and women uniting. When the locals see it, they surround it with rice before digging it up, otherwise it will escape. If a couple is not harmonious, taking it will make them happy. However, when loaded on a river boat, it will sink and cannot cross. The wise use a long line to tie it to the shore, hold the line to board the boat, and then pull it over after crossing. Therefore, it is often found in the areas near the border of Yunnan Province. It is said that those who take it say that a man sees a woman, even if she is Mumu, Xishi and Wang Zhaojun are not as good. A woman sees a man, even if he is ugly, he is like Pan An; even if he is old, he is a strong man.

The above are all original texts from the *Compendium of Materia Medica Supplement*. If Tao Sijin had eaten Parting Love Grass, there would have been no tragedy of two females killing each other. If those who passionately loved Miss Li had eaten Parting Love Grass, there would have been no sudden change of two males killing each other. Moreover, if divorcing men and women who are making a fuss all ate Harmonious Love Grass, they would not file for divorce again, and the careers of copper-plated lawyers would be greatly affected. Can the efficacy of grass and trees be so great and miraculous? I'm afraid it's just a myth of grass and trees.

Metaphor of the Moon 92

— Shi Yan Ye

丨Everything should seek light and perfection丨

The Mid-Autumn Festival moon is the brightest and most perfect, so it is most appreciated. But when we admire the bright and perfect moon, what should we think of our country? The Northeast has been lost for a year, like a moon that is missing and incomplete. We must strive to recover our mountains and rivers, restore our country's glory, and make our four million square miles of territory bright and without blemishes, perfect and without defects, just like the Mid-Autumn Festival moon. We should also think about our country's politics. Today's politics are so dark that there is not a single ray of light, and so fragmented that they are not sound. We must use the power of the people to supervise the government, make politics clear and complete its organization, just like the brightness and perfection of the Mid-Autumn Festival moon, making it lovable. Today's society is also like the political organization, which is poor and unbearably dark. We must use a calm attitude, sharp thinking, and strong will to transform society, making its organization perfect and radiant. People living in this society are happily like dew standing under the Mid-Autumn Festival moon. Throughout history, the national salvation groups have inevitably been full of dark secrets and have not been able to achieve perfect results. How should we soundly organize it in the future? How should we make each heart become a whole? Generate great rays of light and have a harvest with perfect results, and also be like the moon tonight. The brave soldiers who are repeatedly turning over in the Northeast do not have complete weapons and sufficient supplies. There are several hundred people in the east and several thousand people in the west. How imperfect is their battle plan, and how dark and terrible is their future? How should we help them with military supplies and weapons, and give them all kinds of material and spiritual assistance, so that they can shine brightly in the Northeast, sweep away the haze, and achieve perfect results? In short, everything placed before us at present should seek its light and perfection, seeking the light and perfection of tonight's bright moon. The light and perfection of the Mid-Autumn Festival moon are indeed pleasing, and achieving light and perfection in everything at present can make people feel even happier.

Mid-Autumn Festival and the Northeast 93

— Baishi

Incense burners filled with smoke and mist filled the room, which symbolized the righteous army in the Northeast desperately emitting smoke bombs and gunpowder mist to overthrow Japanese imperialism. But thinking that when the incense burners were burned out in the middle of the night, the smoke and mist would disappear, I couldn't help but feel a chill.

Even when the lotus root is broken, the silk remains connected. This is originally a common saying. Unexpectedly, eating lotus root this Mid-Autumn Festival, this saying symbolized the situation in the Northeast. The Manchurian state has been created by the Japanese, but the common people still do not forget their homeland, which is clearly that even when the lotus root is broken, the silk remains connected. But thinking that when putting the lotus root into my mouth, the silk that is still connected must also be broken. I feel even more of a chill.

Mooncakes are an indispensable ornament for the Mid-Autumn Festival, and they can also symbolize China's national power. China is like a whole mooncake. The east is a concession, and the west is a colony, just like being peeled of skin. Now the Japanese simply open their mouths wide and bite off a large piece of the Northeast. The pastry filling is also exposed. Moreover, the Japanese are still drooling over what is left after they bite. Thinking of this, I feel even more apprehensive.

Enjoying Autumn 94

— Qian Taisheng

丨Cut open the mooncake, and leave a corner丨

The young masters and young ladies who have climbed out of the swimming pool are about to try on new autumn clothes. 丨Life is always so fresh, lively, and lovely: in the active and sweet spring, it is always so immersed and washed: the smooth asphalt road is suitable for the Austin cars of 1932 to speed: the major companies with autumn sales are suitable for young ladies and young wives to choose diamond jewelry and dazzling silk fabrics of various colors: what makes the lives of young masters and young ladies more comfortable and richer is the rise of greater department stores and the creation of the world's most modern cinemas: the form of life is always a melody, that is: confusion, decadence, licentiousness, and sinking丨

Autumn has come. In the city, you will not feel the desolation of autumn. If there is, it is only the rushing of autumn festival gifts and the items used for enjoying the Mid-Autumn Festival. That lotus seed paste and mixed nuts Cantonese mooncake, accompanied by the lovely autumn atmosphere under the cool and bright moon, this, together with the young masters and young ladies appreciating the fresh "flowers" in spring, the seven-colored "rainbow" after the summer rain, and the rich poetic atmosphere and the cool feeling that cools the lungs of the "round bright moon" on an autumn night, this should make people forget thousands of times of troubles and ten thousand times of sorrows丨

But, cut open the mooncake, and leave a corner丨That quarter of the Northeast that has been seized, under the "round bright moon" shining on the 30 million compatriots outside the customs who are shedding tears and fighting to the death, when you are eating coconut, mixed nuts, and ham mooncakes, to commemorate the tragic pain of your 30 million compatriots locked up outside the customs, I hope you will leave a corner for them as a memorial of mourning丨

The bright moon is lovely, and the Northeast is even more lovely丨One-quarter of the land, our 30 million compatriots丨

Cut open the mooncake, and leave a corner丨

Silver Thread of the Rotary Club Fiction (14) 95

— Jiang Hongjiao

(7)

"Then you became a regiment commander," you must be very happy now; perhaps your hometown and everything from the past are no longer valuable, causing you to occasionally reminisce?"

"What! As long as I have a breath of life, I will not forget the traces of the past; as long as I have a little bit of inspiration, I am always thinking about how to make my dear Fenruo happy. You should know how uncomfortable I was in my heart the day you decided to marry. But I didn't want to learn the cowardice of ordinary people by swallowing sleeping pills or jumping into the sea to commit suicide. I only thought about how to punish you so that at some point, in some environment, you would feel that marrying this battalion commander was completely wrong, and that adapting to the demands and expectations of your family was also a huge fallacy. I still trust myself. I am definitely not a schoolteacher in the making. I can definitely be like the Chinese saying, 'mount the horse to kill bandits, dismount the horse to draft proclamations'; or like the divine bravery of medieval Western knights, or within a certain period of time, snatch you to my place from your husband's hands. Alas, I was so indignant at the time, and the blood in my whole body was boiling. And you, you were enjoying the happiness of your new marriage, with another man leaning on you and embracing you. How would you know that your sinner had abandoned everything and fled to the army?"

"Yes, this is my fault, and also my misfortune. But now, everything is over. Besides praying that you will always be happy and fulfill your responsibilities to the country and the people, I have no other thoughts."

"Then you have no regrets about living this kind of life?"

"I can't blame anyone anymore. Blaming my own fate is also meaningless. Beautiful youth, like flowing water, has already passed. I don't plan to ask for anything more before I breathe my last."

"But if you don't ask for anything, doesn't that mean I'm not allowed to have any wishes?"

"Of course, this is an exception. You should have bigger wishes: a lovely wife, smart children, work that will shock the whole world

and save all of mankind from depravity. You should wish for it, you should achieve your goals. But you shouldn't come here again, to meet your former unfortunate friend."

"Can't you make your thoughts more beautiful, the same as before? Can't you make your life more joyful, surpassing the past and the present? My indignation from the past has now turned into earnest longing. I am willing to forget all the old hatred, but I don't want to forget the passion you had for me. I don't believe your youth has passed. What I see before me is still the beautiful Fenruo from thirteen years ago. I don't want you to suffer for the rest of your life, living with a madman forever, I don't want you to embroider wedding dresses for other people's daughters forever. I want to see you embraced by me, embroidering a wedding dress for yourself for my sake."

"Alas, please forgive me. Although I only married for two months before my husband died, leaving me lonely and desolate until now, the families and relatives of the two families in between have slowly died, leaving only a bored and immortal me. But I want to save someone before I die. That person is that madman. Poor thing, he is also a pitiful wretch. Please allow me, don't oppose me or deprive me of my will. But your affection, I will take to my coffin and be eternally grateful for."

Commercial News

Financial and Gold Markets React and Fall Back 96

Falling back by more than five taels, yesterday's gold auction market showed a reaction and fell. There were some twists and turns in between, but the overall market did not fall back by more than four taels. Looking back, the near and far months of the overseas silver market uniformly reported contractions. However, the price of gold was just the opposite. It initially fell, because the footing of the silver bars was not good. The United States posted a premium of 125 or more after the market closed, as if there were buyers. Therefore, the market turned firm, which affected it. The psychology of the industry tended to weaken. Afterwards, because the swap had already started, the exchange was based on the level of the discount. However, with a rise and fall of two or three taels, the foreign exchange deviated, and short positions were seen, making the market even more lackluster. Because of Wednesday, the agents of each gold firm had previously requested the exchange to close the market, but were not allowed. Although the exchange issued another notice yesterday advising them to operate as usual, the representatives would not rest until their goal was achieved, so they did not open the market. However, they all arrived at the exchange at 4:30 PM as scheduled, and then dispersed. The swap starts on the 16th of each month, but each firm must start one day earlier. However, the 15th was a holiday for the Mid-Autumn Festival according to the lunar calendar, so trading only started yesterday morning. The discount was still posted by the short side, initially four taels to 3.8 taels. Then, because the bulls were unwilling to lightly swap, it was pushed up to 6.89 taels to seven taels, and finally returned to 5.5 taels, with a little more than six taels. It is said that most of the major bulls did not take action, but there were quite a few transactions. Shaoxing Autumn Cocoons Have the Lowest Drying Loss 109

Nansha Model Silk-producing Area Only Yields Slightly More Than 300 Jin

Nansha in Shaoxing has been designated as a model silk-producing area by the Zhejiang Construction Department. It has a guidance center, and all procedures such as seed distribution, disinfection, egg incubation, and mulberry feeding are conducted under the supervision of instructors. Therefore, the results are the best. The new cocoon harvest is about 80% of a normal year. The fresh cocoons collected by the autumn cocoon production and sales cooperative are currently being dried in order, and the drying loss is the lowest. On average, 306 jin of fresh cocoons can be dried into 100 jin of dry cocoons. Other reports indicate a drying loss requiring 312 jin.

Discourse

Social Parasites 112

— Parasite

In the issue of the 本埠 supplement of our newspaper on September 7th, Mr. Quan's cartoon depicted a monk sitting in lotus position, chanting and tapping a wooden fish, with the inscription "Social Parasite" above it. After seeing it, I couldn't help but feel the need to speak out on behalf of the monks. It's not because I sympathize with their reliance on alms for sustenance, nor am I advocating for them or righting wrongs. However, because Mr. Quan used the phrase "social parasite," I felt that his criticism was somewhat biased. The parasites in China are not limited to monks, and among monks, there are producers as well. Now, let me just talk about Shanghai. Generally speaking, those who live in Western-style houses, eat fancy meals, and ride in cars, loafing around all day without doing anything, as well as those who want to work but society doesn't give them the opportunity, driving the strong to robbery and the weak to begging, are not under discussion. I'm just asking, from the highest-ranking government official to the lowest street vendor, who is a producer? If we consider these people to be non-producers, then what should we call them? Aren't they social parasites? Moreover, apart from low-level clerks and rickshaw pullers, their lives are much more comfortable than those of the hardworking farmers and laborers who toil day and night. I don't know the exact population of Shanghai, and I certainly can't give you an accurate proportion of parasites to those being parasitized, but based on the current situation, I can boldly assert that the ratio is almost one to one hundred: "99 parasites for every 1 person being parasitized." Furthermore, these high-level parasites not only don't produce themselves, but they also desperately consume goods from abroad, "buying foreign goods," making it impossible for the producing compatriots being parasitized to survive. Isn't this a desire for mutual destruction?

My humble article is not intended to criticize Mr. Quan's cartoon for being incorrect. It's just that Mr. Quan's inscription "social parasite" aroused a social concept in my chest that I had long wanted to express but hadn't yet. (Payment received)

Literature and Art

Zheng Jicheng Assassinated Zhang Zongchang 113

— Yun Jianliang

The New Double-Reed Puppet State 114

The arch-villain shouldn't think he can escape the law, the sound of gunfire leaves no possibility for peace. A Kun, a gangster on the blacklist (When Zhang arrived in Suzhou, a certain unemployed ironsmith from Wuxi who had old acquaintanceship with him, waited for him to emerge, and loudly called out "Brother A Kun," whereupon he was given a military position), Old Zheng's long-held grudge is now settled, all the Shandong compatriots cheer. The young man's heroic spirit soars into the clouds. The warlords should realize, that their corpses will be exposed and their souls will find no place to reside.

Not avenging one's parents is unthinkable, a man's ambition should be as steadfast as gold. The remaining mountains and waters bring sorrow to the three provinces, blood and tears flow, bearing a year of suffering. Precisely when the hero sheds his red blood, the father's grudge can be avenged in the afterlife. The Zheng family has a son who can fight for what's right, quickly strike the whip to make amends for past omissions.

Science

A Discussion on Four-Dimensional Space (Continued) 115

From this perspective, time and space are indeed equally important.

Now, let me give a few more examples to illustrate this four-dimensional space.

We hardly ever see things in one-dimensional space. However, I once heard a story like this: A mantis was walking on the road. Suddenly, a general's car came from ahead, but it still bravely moved forward without yielding. So, it sacrificed itself. This story was originally about the bravery of the mantis, but perhaps it was because the mantis didn't have a sufficient understanding of two- or three-dimensional space.

Regarding two-dimensional space, I remember an ancient saying: "Draw a circle as a prison." That is to say, if you just draw a circle around someone who has committed a mistake, he will stay there forever. This shows the honesty of the ancients. However, when we think carefully about it, perhaps it was due to the simplicity of their thinking. They only knew about two-dimensional space and hadn't yet discovered or had a sufficient understanding of three-dimensional space.

Page 21

As for three-dimensional space, our lives are in three-dimensional space.

The Chinese do not yet have a sufficient understanding of four-dimensional space.

I once heard a joke like this: A person was walking on the road and suddenly encountered heavy rain. But he still strolled along slowly. Someone asked him why he didn't run faster. His reply was that it was raining ahead too, so what was the point of running faster.

After hearing such a story, we certainly can't say that he is a fool. There is indeed philosophy in his words. There is nothing wrong with his words, but we can only say that he doesn't have a sufficient understanding of four-dimensional space.

The Chinese do indeed lack an understanding of four-dimensional space. Even in terms of language, the languages of England, France, and Germany all have a sense of time, but Chinese does not.

Chinese people are often late for meetings. This may also be proof of this.

Now, the fifth dimension is about to be discovered. China, which is lagging behind in science, should at least have a sufficient awareness of four-dimensional space.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Suggestions for Improving Accounting 116

— Jiang Jirong

Accounting scholars study the principles of bookkeeping using scientific methods. Few Chinese shops and factories adopt modern accounting; even fewer use semi-modern methods. The vast majority of businesses still use the old-fashioned single-entry accounting to record their daily transactions. I recall countless cases where Chinese shops faced various problems due to unclear bookkeeping, leading to embezzlement. There are also countless instances where factory products failed to compete due to inaccurate cost calculations. Furthermore, on the household level, countless families have been bankrupted due to a lack of budgeting beforehand and no final accounting afterward. At this time when the nation is in trouble and commerce and industry are declining, and when various industries are laying off employees, it is all the more important to promote domestic goods and improve accounting practices. Moreover, under party rule, economic transparency has become a precedent. If we don't improve quickly and continue with the old ways, how can we compete successfully? How can the economy be transparent? How can families be prosperous? Here are a few suggestions for reference:

(1) In current social organizations, accounting positions are often filled by relatives or friends. Even those who hire accountants for audits often do so merely to avoid external advice. Therefore, accountants should conduct thorough reviews and detailed reports with a spirit of impartiality and selflessness. Do not let the public lose faith, as this would hinder the progress of the accounting profession.

(2) China is a world marketplace, and the competition is fierce. China's industry is still in its infancy. The government offers little promotion or protection, making it difficult to compete with foreign businesses. At this time of promoting domestic goods, Chinese merchants should improve their products and offer lower prices, striving for "low prices and good quality" to appeal to the masses. Modern cost accounting is essential for accurately calculating costs, allowing for reasonable profits even with the lowest selling price. Therefore, it is not only necessary for Chinese factories and businesses to adopt modern accounting, but larger factories should also establish cost accounting research departments to lower costs and reduce selling prices. Sales will increase accordingly, and domestic production will be promoted, with predictable results.

(3) The Institute of Certified Public Accountants, as the hub for the study of accounting, should regularly publish materials related to accounting for commercial reference and encouragement. Accountants should not raise their fees too high and should offer reasonable prices to promote widespread adoption.

(4) Schools, as the breeding ground for future talents, should add bookkeeping and accounting courses to meet social needs. Shops and factories should employ as many graduates as possible to facilitate improvement and progress. This is also important on the household level.

(5) Chambers of Commerce in various cities should also hire accountants or jointly discuss accounting issues with the Institute of Certified Public Accountants, allowing merchants to understand the principles and benefits of modern accounting. They should also provide guidance from time to time to promote improvement. If this can be done, the effect will be even greater.

School Scene

A Middle School Student 117

— Wu Wei

This semester, there is a new face in our classroom. His face is painted as white as lime, just missing a touch of rouge and lipstick, otherwise he would almost look like a woman. He has so much perfume on him that the fragrance is overwhelming, truly a fop. He says he used to study at S University and was about to graduate, but because he needs a middle school diploma, he asked our principal's brother-in-law to introduce him.

This "ass-kisser" (the nickname given to him by the classmates) doesn't take studying seriously. He has probably forgotten the original intention of coming to school, so he only attends a maximum of two hours of class each day. However, there is one thing that many classmates admire about him: no matter how much he cuts class, his name never appears on the list of absentees.

He wastes his time like this every day. He comes back from outside (the dance hall) at six o'clock in the morning and goes to bed. He doesn't get up until half past ten, so he never attends the two classes from nine to eleven, except for the one day of formal lessons... He manages to sit in the classroom for the eleven to twelve class, but he either reads the newspaper or novels, rarely paying attention to the textbooks. As soon as he hears the dismissal bell, he is the first one out of the classroom!

Although he boards at the school, he is never seen in the dining hall. However, he can be found at XX Restaurant across from the school gate. (Of course! How could the school's food suit the taste of a young master like him?)

He seems to be able to force himself to attend the one to two class. But after two o'clock, he never comes back to the classroom. According to L, who lives in the room next to him, there is a singing tutor who brings a bird master to sing "The Female Escort" etc. from half past two. Most inexplicably, the dorm supervisor seems to be deaf at this time, not saying a word. Anyway, if any other dorm did that, he would interfere. In this respect, I must admit that this "ass-kisser" has great influence. After three o'clock, a fashionable girl comes to find him every day, and then they go out together, not returning until dawn.

Alas! This kind of student doesn't sincerely come to study, perhaps he's just using it as a front? And the school authorities can actually tolerate this social parasite. It's really a strange thing. Alas, education, education, actually educates such students!

End of Complaint

Planting Children 118

— Shi Ben

The day before yesterday, on my way home from the office, I walked into the lane and saw many women standing in front of the Zhang family's door, talking and whispering. Everyone's eyes were all directed inside, as if there was some good show to watch, attracting so much attention from the public. Out of curiosity, I walked over to take a look and saw an old woman in her fifties sitting in the middle of the Zhang family's living room. Judging by her appearance, she was wearing a blue cotton single-layer shirt that reached past her knees, shoes with red cloth heel pulls, and a pair of round earrings as big as copper coins on her ears. Her hair was styled in a high, ingot-shaped bun on top of her head. From her strange eighteenth-century attire, I knew that she was one of the gossiping women. Five or six young women were sitting around her, all leaning their ears to listen quietly to what she was saying. Zhang's mother's eldest daughter-in-law was talking to her intently. "Granny! I've already had my bazi calculated, and I understand the problem. It's destined in my fate to have children, but will I have good news this year? Well, let me ask the Lingguan to see," the old woman said, reaching into her arms and taking out a wooden puppet about an inch long, placing it next to her ear, as if listening to the telephone. She continued, "The Lingguan says that your fate is to have children late. You'll have to wait until you're thirty-eight, still ten years away."

"Old woman! In that case, please ask the Lingguan again, is there any way to think of?" Zhang's eldest daughter-in-law was eager to have children and didn't care how embarrassed she was, saying this. But her snow-white face was already blushing.

"..." The old woman's lips trembled and moved, as if murmuring some incantation. The wooden puppet in her hand kept being stuffed to her ear for a kiss. After a while, she said, "The Lingguan has already said that it's good to plant one with you. But you need to donate four yuan for incense and candles... He told me to give you eight Qilin Sending Son pills. On the lower half of the night of the Mid-Autumn Festival in August, use boiling water to mix it with incense ash and drink it. At that time, the Lingguan will be secretly planting a white and fat official with you."

"Ah! Grandma! The price is too high, can you reduce it a bit?" Zhang's eldest daughter-in-law, wants to raise a son, but finds the money a bit painful.

"Grandma! You don't understand. This money is not for me, it's for the Lingguan to buy incense and candles. Don't say it anymore. The Lingguan never goes back on his word!" the old woman said in a way that there was absolutely no bargaining,

"In that case... I will pay you four yuan, but please ask the Lingguan to make it faster..." Zhang's eldest daughter-in-law, became embarrassed at this point, and stopped talking. She hastily reached into her pocket and took out four silver dollars, handing them to the old woman.

"Don't worry, Grandma. We always do things properly. I guarantee that by this time next year, you will be holding a little official in your hands. At that time, I will come to have a cup of wedding wine!" the old woman said, with a smile all over her face, showing a victorious mood. She stuffed the four old dollars into her arms while saying this.

"Lingguan... Plant a white and fat official... Incense candles... X dollars..." In an instant, such a sound came from the Yang family's living room in the west lane.

No Way Out

Meiying 119

— Ren Ze

Meiying had to drop out of school because of financial reasons. Seeing her classmates happily carrying their schoolbags to school, she was left at home to live a lonely life. But it would have been nice if she could have lived comfortably at home. Because driven by bread, the whip of life hit her back again and again, she had to force herself to embark on the road to earning a living.

Her mother found her a job as a factory worker in a tobacco company.

When she went to work for the first time in the morning, she carried a food basket and walked out of the door. How ashamed she was! Because she was afraid of meeting acquaintances, she had to lower her head and walk on quiet roads.

At the factory, because Meiying was a novice, she was inevitably ridiculed by the foreman and the other female workers. Even when other people were joking, Meiying thought they were mocking her.

At mealtime, Meiying opened her food basket. A bowl of rice and a bowl of vegetables. When Meiying saw it, she couldn't help but feel a pang in her heart and secretly shed a few tears. Afraid of being seen, she had to wipe her eyes and force herself to eat a few mouthfuls of rice, then re-cover the food basket.

Woo, woo, woo! The whistle blew three times, and the workers were released. Many people were crowding and walking out. Meiying also followed inside.

On the road, she walked with sadness. Walking and walking, she unknowingly arrived at the Bund. She thought, "Eh! How did I get here? Ah! It's really heartbreaking! How much did my father and mother love me? Now, driven by the whip of life, I have to show my face and do this kind of work, and I have to be laughed at. Ah! Ah! In this world, where can I find sympathy? Tomorrow, the day after tomorrow, I will suffer the same embarrassment. What am I going to do?"

Thinking of this, her tears welled up like a spring, dripping all over her clothes, dripping on the ground.

For a long time, she stopped being sad, and turned around and thought, "Ah! What's there to be nostalgic for in this world? It's better to die cleanly. Even my father and mother can reduce a lot of pain."

After thinking, she put down her food basket and threw herself into the river.

The waters of the Huangpu flowed, flowed, swallowed Meiying, only raised a few whirlpools, and flowed as usual forever.

A Corner of Society

About the Beggar's Mistress 120

— Jun Heng

Because of reproduction and sexual needs, it is of course unavoidable for everyone. However, a beggar who has no food or clothing and already has a wife, also wants to learn from the wealthy officials and get a mistress. This is something that must be recorded.

A friend of mine runs a small grocery store on Lujiabang Road. I often go there to chat. Next door to them is a low bungalow, which is also the residence of beggars. Yesterday, while I was chatting with my friend, there was a loud bang, which was the sound of a teacup breaking. Then three ragged men and women, tangled together, were pushed out of the low bungalow. A woman in her forties pointed at the woman in her thirties, whose nose was bleeding, and cursed: "You rotten thing, I have been his wife for more than ten years, and we have always been very harmonious. Ever since you bewitched him, he abandoned me. Today, I must tear your thing apart!" She pounced on her and grabbed the hair of the woman in her thirties, and kicked the man with her foot. Later, they were finally persuaded to stop by their neighbors. This storm in a vinegar sea finally calmed down.

My friend said: The man puts red candle oil and flour on his rotten leg every day, dresses up and goes to the streets to beg for money. He always gets two or three strings of cash. The woman in her thirties also goes to various lanes to pretend to be looking for her husband, crying and looking very pitiful, so sometimes she can still cheat three or four yuan a day. She is the woman he recently took as a mistress, considered his concubine. The woman in her forties, is the first wife, goes to beg people to sue for money. My friend also said: my little grocery store is really not as good as them, they are even lending money at high interest!

"Hmm, this deformed society!" I couldn't help but sigh. (Payment received)

Police Department sues Yan Ziqing et al. regarding opium (Main Text): Yan Ziqing, as a recidivist, is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for providing a building for others to smoke opium substitutes for profit. Zhang Fusheng, as a recidivist, is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. Hu Peibo is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. The number of days of pre-trial detention for all shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. Hu Peibo is given a three-year suspended sentence. The smoking paraphernalia is confiscated according to the list.

Police Department sues Yu Huang et al. regarding opium (Main Text): Yu Huang is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing a building for others to smoke opium substitutes for profit. Yu Kangbo and Zhang Hai are each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. The number of days of pre-trial detention for all shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. Yu Huang and Yu Kangbo are given a three-year suspended sentence. The smoking paraphernalia and red pills are confiscated according to the list.

Police Department sues Li Azhang regarding opium (Main Text): Li Azhang is fined twenty yuan for possessing opium. If the fine is converted to imprisonment, it shall be at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of pre-trial detention is counted as two yuan per day. A small package of opium is confiscated and burned.

Police Department sues Li Ahong et al. for gang robbery (Main Text): Li Ahong, along with three or more persons, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for recidivist robbery with weapons. Ye Amao is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for robbery with weapons committed by a group of three or more. Liu Guisheng and Jiang Debao are each sentenced to eight years of imprisonment for robbery with weapons committed by a group of three or more. Qian Jinshan and Jin Rensheng are each sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment for robbery with weapons committed by a group of three or more. The number of days of pre-trial detention for all shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. Zhu Yaxian, Zhou Xinyu, Wu Qichang, and He Sifu are found not guilty. One handgun and six bullets are confiscated.

Police Department sues Zhang Moyun for theft (Main Text): Zhang Moyun is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for theft and two months of imprisonment for attempted fraud. The executed sentence is three months of imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be counted as one day for every two days of imprisonment. Zhang Moyun shall return 58.50 yuan to Jin Guangming.

Police Department sues Ding Wang regarding opium (Main Text): Ding Wang is fined thirty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If unable to pay the fine, she will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of pre-trial detention is counted as two yuan per day of the fine. One opium pipe, two opium lamps, three opium needles, one opium tray, and five small boxes of opium paste are confiscated and burned.

Police Department sues Wang Xiangbai regarding opium (Main Text): Wang Xiangbai is fined forty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If unable to pay the fine, he will be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of pre-trial detention is counted as two yuan per day of the fine. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium needle, one opium tray, and twenty opium bubbles are confiscated and burned. (Above, September 14)

Jiangsu Higher Court, Third Branch 123

In the case of a commission and damages dispute between Hulins Silk Weaving Co., Ltd., etc., and the French firm Xue Jialai, the court rules as follows (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The costs of the second-instance litigation shall be borne by the appellant.
